permissions through middleware, and manage folder/dashboard inheritance. Here are the key architectural components:\\n\\n**Role Definitions (Tier 1):**\\nThe three-tier organization roles are defined in `pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go` as a RoleType enum with four values: RoleNone, RoleViewer, RoleEditor, and RoleAdmin. Each role has a defined precedence order (None=10, Viewer=20, Editor=30, Admin=40) used for permission inheritance. These constants are re-exported in `pkg/services/org/model.go` for use throughout the codebase.\\n\\n**Role-to-Permission Mapping (Tier 2):**\\nThe mapping between organization roles and specific RBAC permissions is built in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` through the `BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()` function, which creates basic role definitions (basic:viewer, basic:editor, basic:admin) with empty permission lists that are later populated. Specific dashboard and folder roles are registered in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go` and `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go` through `registerDashboardRoles()` and `registerFolderRoles()` functions, which define:\\n- DashboardViewActions (read dashboards, read annotations)\\n- DashboardEditActions (view + write dashboards, delete dashboards, manage annotations)\\n- DashboardAdminActions (edit + read/write permissions)\\n- FolderViewActions (read folders, read alerts, read library panels)\\n- FolderEditActions (view + write folders, create dashboards, create/manage alerts)\\n- FolderAdminActions (edit + read/write folder permissions)\\n\\nThese are registered via `accesscontrol.RoleRegistration` with Grants to the appropriate org roles. The actual permissions are stored in the database and seeded by `pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/basic_role_db_seed.go` through the `refreshBasicRolePermissionsInDB()` function.\\n\\n**Permission Guard Middleware (Tier 3):**\\nPermission enforcement occurs through middleware defined in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`. The `Middleware()` function wraps HTTP handlers with an `Evaluator`, and the `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware()` function creates organization-scoped authorization gates. Both use the `authorize()` function which evaluates permissions against a user's claims via the AccessControl service's `Evaluate()` method, comparing against scoped RBAC permissions (actions with resource scopes like \\\"dashboards:uid:abc123\\\").\\n\\n**Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance:**\\nFolder and dashboard permissions are managed by `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/service.go`, which provides a generic `Service` with `GetPermissions()` and `SetPermissions()` methods. Inheritance is handled through the `InheritedScopesSolver` callback, which is implemented in `pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go` via the `GetInheritedScopes()` function. This function retrieves parent folder UIDs using `folderService.GetParents()` and generates inherited scopes (e.g., folder:uid:parent1, folder:uid:parent2) so that a user's folder-level permissions cascade to nested dashboards and subfolders.\\n\\nDashboard-specific inherited scopes are resolved through `NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver()` and `NewDashboardIDScopeResolver()` in the same file, which include both the dashboard scope and its parent folder scope hierarchy. When a dashboard is accessed, the permission check includes scopes for the dashboard, its containing folder, and all ancestor folders up the tree, enabling permission inheritance from parent folders.\\n\\n**HTTP API and Service Integration:**\\nThe HTTP API for managing permissions is exposed in `pkg/api/accesscontrol.go` (which declares fixed roles), `pkg/api/dashboard.go`, and `pkg/api/folder.go` (which handle permission checks on API endpoints). The dashboard service in `pkg/services/dashboards/service/dashboard_service.go` uses the `getPermissionsService()` method to route permission operations to either `folderPermissions` or `dashboardPermissions` service instances registered from the OSS access control implementations.\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go`: Defines Permission, RoleDTO, and related data structures\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/authorizer.go`: Implements the Authorize interface for permission evaluation\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard.go`: Implements permission filtering in SQL queries for dashboard access control\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/folders/folder_storage.go`: Sets default folder permissions on creation\\n- `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go`: Implements folder-level permission checks including inherited permissions\\n\\nThis architecture ensures that the three-tier permission model is consistently enforced across all dashboard and folder operations, with permissions inherited from parent folders and mediated through RBAC action/scope evaluation.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3912,"cache_read_input_tokens":101119,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3912},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"87f46ab2-3735-489d-8f1a-0ee1c3cb6f83","uuid":"117768c9-75ff-43e5-b975-71c907c1c34a"}
